if (is_file('update/vnag_framework.inc.php') && (sha1_file('update/vnag_framework.inc.php') != 'f592114b0ac505598cb5875da26570bcee25ef4e')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: update/vnag_framework.inc.php');
	$tmp = pathinfo('update/vnag_framework.inc.php');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/vnag_framework.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('update/vnag_framework.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}

	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/vnag_framework.inc.php');

	warn('Could not change file permissions of update/vnag_framework.inc.php');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'ff21fb6e9514841bb5b544f107b5836213fb1b2a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ff21fb6e9514841bb5b544f107b5836213fb1b2a') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '16d8da61f23598c79127a077ef9c249ecaf70fa4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ff21fb6e9514841bb5b544f107b5836213fb1b2a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') != '85e84e02754f455e8aa77ec4131721a62a63831c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '85e84e02754f455e8aa77ec4131721a62a63831c') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '823223eda6f564f72e41ae200eafcb2aa63030ad') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '85e84e02754f455e8aa77ec4131721a62a63831c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: update/index.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != '27c60e9234ba459d51dcb4b93b7aa7fb0e3c0cc6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '27c60e9234ba459d51dcb4b93b7aa7fb0e3c0cc6') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '175f51939b9b4f6cfc3d2f9469556a4ea21b14c5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '27c60e9234ba459d51dcb4b93b7aa7fb0e3c0cc6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 165\n");

echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
